Finance

The Exchange Market Turns Firm

The Standard Gold Price Falls 6.6 Yuan

Rumors After Closing Suggesting the Bullish Trend Has Not DimINIshed

After the gold market experienced a surprising surge recently, the market fell back yesterday. However, investor confidence remains high, and the bullish trend persists. There were many interruptions during the day. During this time of extreme financial tightness, bullish rumors resurfaced, and the upward trend resumed after the close. Initially in the morning, overseas silver markets in both England and the United States contracted. However, major players said that the United States had bought forward silver at the close, with the Montevideo forward silver price contracting by between 0.06 and 0.09. Exchange rates continued to fall, and London spot gold rose by 7.5 pence. People were uneasy about inflation. Mr. Mau was already denying that the news was spreading. Off-market trading was rumored to be around 98.89, which was relatively stable compared to the previous day's close. However, major players such as Fuyong, Yuan Maoyong, Fufu, and Ren Fayong sold and forecast a fall. The Central Bank's posted rates revealed that the pound was flat and the U.S. dollar contracted by 0.0625. The customs gold unit rose by 0.01. The standard gold price was 1004.6 yuan, which had little impact, and investor confidence was slightly weak. After opening, major players continued to offer, and prices gradually fell. However, due to investor uneasiness, there were frequent interruptions after prices fell. The situation was uncertain, and investor confidence remained bullish. Later, demand from major players exceeded supply. It was learned that the HSBC posted rates would reveal that the pound was flat and the U.S. dollar contracted by 0.0625, which would still be able to boost prices. When prices opened, because the quotation for foreign wheat was low, both inside and outside the industry took a wait-and-see attitude. Therefore, the initial market was loose and uneventful. Subsequently, trading in various sessions remained weak. However, as factories did not sell off aggressively, the market remained buoyant. When the market opened in the afternoon, the market slightly picked up. Due to hedging and tight supply this month, out-of-town merchants had slight demand, and prices stabilized. For longer-term months, out-of-industry buying remained active, and prices gradually increased. As monthly exchange rates frequently contracted, ordering spot wheat inevitably caused further anxiety. As a result, this month was slightly better by 0.005 yuan, January was better by 0.0125 yuan, February was better by 0.015 yuan, March was better by 0.0175 yuan, April was better by 0.02 yuan, and May was better by 0.0175 yuan.

Year-End Approaching

Futures Wheat Market Inactive

Yesterday, after the futures wheat market opened in the morning and afternoon, prices for various months generally remained flat and weak. With the quotation of foreign wheat, Chicago fell by about 0.04, 0.05, and 0.06 yuan, and Canada fell by 0.03 and 0.04 yuan. After quotations, trading in various months remained inactive, and prices fluctuated little. In the afternoon sessions, the current month initially fell by 0.03 and 0.04 yuan due to approaching delivery. However, it then slightly improved. Quotations for longer-term months remained low. Selling was limited because settlement was approaching, and there was no aggressive trading inside or outside the market. As a result, this month was slightly down by 0.005 yuan, January and February were down by 0.01 yuan, and March was better by 0.01 yuan. In the spot wheat market, there was a slight increase in trading, and prices also rose slightly by 0.01 or 0.02 yuan. Shandong wheat opened at 4.06 yuan, and Xuzhou Yao wheat opened at 4.03 yuan. Shen Da and Hua Feng each purchased 1,000 bags.

Chicago Wheat Prices have fallen as they approach import benchmarks, southwest weather has improved, and foreign news is weak, causing further weakness.

Rice Prices in Hexia Unchanged

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, a total of forty ships arrived from various sources (with a total of 70 shi of goods). The market improved due to the major festivities. However, there were instances of chaos, resulting in an inconsistent overall picture. If each evening, Qing Baowei continued to sell 700 to 800 bags, prices rebounded by several fen to a jiao. Thick Japonica also saw prices rise by several fen to a chi. Subsequently, the market situation will depend on weather conditions. Varieties such as Duyangjian and Yinyuan remained stable.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, thirty to forty firms from various sources along the river and inland. There are one hundred ships in the river. Spot sales of Bai Jing did not only improve in the early market, but also shifted in the noon market. High-quality Bai Yuan sales were active, while average quality was flat. Early Bo Dao and other small grain varieties sold well. The market trend for Bai Jing weakened in the early market by several fen to nearly a jiao. The later market stabilized, and Bai Yuan prices increased several times. Early Bo Dao prices remained stable, and Yang Jian weakened. Du Jian and Bu Jian were similar, while Ji Jian was slightly tight.

Foreign Rice Flat, Ke Xian Good

𨗴 Rice Continues to Arrive

Yesterday, the foreign rice market initially showed a mixed trend. Subsequently, foreign merchants offered February small-package rice at 4.84 yuan, while March回笼 small-package rice was initially offered at 4.88 yuan. Today, Shantaitex万丰 and others sold at slightly lower prices. By the afternoon, as exchange rates contracted, the 4.84 yuan February small-package offer failed to materialize, and market sentiment stabilized again. Currently, 2,200 bags of machine-milled rice and 200 bags of broken rice were purchased by local businesses at slightly lower prices. The成交 of 900 tons of回笼期 rice. Yesterday,客秈 was active in Shazhe, and the local market was also good, with excellent market conditions. However, as the inland market stalled, prices also rose slightly.

The foreign rice ordered by this city continues to arrive in Shanghai. It is estimated that 16,500 bags of 𨗴 rice loaded on the Norwegian ship Harvard were sunk in the Huangpu River the day before yesterday. Salvage operations are underway. It is also reported that the ship Andelabon from the French company is arriving in Shanghai today, carrying 19,000 bags of rice, which is scheduled to be stored in the Zhaoshangju Central Warehouse.

Sugar Market

New Branch Red Opens at Thirteen Yuan

Yesterday, the sugar market trend was slightly better. The association's price range for #4 raw sugar spot was 18.45 yuan, up 0.05 yuan from the previous day.转口货 was quoted at 5 yuan. Number 19 red sugar was 14.5 yuan, up 0.01 yuan. Ordinary Numbers 8 and 9 were quoted at 14 yuan. 转口货 was quoted at 5 yuan. Taikoo sugar and the factory's cotton-bleached sugar remained unchanged. The first batch of domestic new Shimen slices arrived in 100 bags and were immediately opened for sale at 11 yuan. 17 bags of New Branch Red arrived and opened at 14 yuan. Prices for New Chao Qing have recently fallen in the Shanghai market and may ease, but yesterday's news indicated that prices are tightening again in Shishi as shipments to Shantou are gradually decreasing due to the need to sell at a loss in the current market. Furthermore, sales here are strong, and the future market is unlikely to ease.

The import of sugar into this port has historically been dominated by Japan and Holland. However, imports from Japan have recently decreased slightly. The Dutch sugar, transported on the Java ship Zhizhibaide, which arrived the day before yesterday (17th), carried a large quantity of 30,000 bags.

Zhabei Goods

Jinshan Branch Market Softens

Sales within the Jinshan Branch are sluggish, and the market has declined. There is no formal price, and the prices for small-lot transactions by trading houses have also softened significantly. For example, ordinary goods, even the better ones, are priced at no more than 30 yuan. Lower quality goods are even less. Sales are even more chaotic. However, market prices at this point may stabilize.

Free Talk

Our Era and Literature

— Di Zhou

Let us try to open our eyes and see how humanity's entire life in this era—social, cultural—is churning in a universal torrent! Let us try to quietly trace the history of the past; I fear we cannot find a state of life as rich and vigorous as the present! The simplest example is: on any given day, we know how humans are racking their brains and exhausting their strength—either large-scale production and construction are completed, or most production mechanisms go bankrupt, or valuable scientific inventions succeed, and finally, or the execution of battles—wars, military expansion, negotiations, disturbances...

These can all be reported to us by daily newspapers and magazines. Even though in this kaleidoscopic phenomenon, the joy and sorrow given to people are unequal, and the influences and effects given to people are different, we cannot but say: This era is a great era unprecedented in history, no matter from which aspect!

In this way, what kind of development can the literature of this era have? This is a question worth examining, and at the same time, it is a question that must be raised and answered for modern literary youths.

From the historian's perspective, the tragedies of ancient Greece could only be produced in the balanced and sophisticated slave culture of that time. Only under the conditions of the high development of handicraft and commercial capital in England in the late sixteenth century could English culture be rapidly improved, and Shakespeare's national treasure-like dramas appear. Critics have not erased personal genius, but personal genius exists in society. Therefore, the production of brilliant art and great works is only possible under appropriate social conditions. Furthermore, different social situations and conditions produce different art or works. The difference between Shakespeare's tragedies and ancient Greek tragedies is an illustration of the latter point. "The Iron Flood," "Cement," and "The Rout" are famous works that could only be produced after the end of military affairs, which is the best example of the former point.

So, what are the social conditions of this era? What kind of development conditions does the current social image provide for literature? We can examine it from two aspects.

First: The current social images reflect the entirety of humanity's rational content to the highest degree. Old appearances from ancient times to the present, as well as new postures that were only prototypes in modern times and are now surging forward, all exist simultaneously with flesh and blood. The "sublimity" of mankind in the play "Antigone" that Hegel repeatedly praised, the unfolding of an entire era in Tolstoy's works that Vladimir longed for, etc., are now presented to people in a more vast, profound, and insightful manner. This is to say that the reality of this era provides literature with an incomparably rich content. With its developing melody and tremors, it not only extracts the "ordinary" materials all over the mountains and valleys but also extraordinarily indicates the central content where the "meaning" lies. From this point of view, the surroundings of this era provide materials for great literary content that were not available before. Isn't it true that serious people are absorbing these materials, organizing these materials, and nurturing them into the brilliant light like the rising sun of the Soviet Union, Japan, Germany...?

Second: The exploration of new literary frontiers has, up to now, left behind many monuments that shake the souls of people in this era. These, at least, exist as signposts for the pioneers of contemporary literature, radiating light. Generally speaking, we now have the conditions for great creation. From ideological criticism to the application of new techniques, there are many models and sufficient experience. However, these conditions show differences in degree due to the different historical developments in various regions. For example, China's current "this kind of" situation cannot be said to be a suitable condition for producing great works. Even so, the existence of that condition is an undeniable fact. The era is demanding the production of great works. It has provided all the things needed for great works and is looking forward to it. But it also spreads many difficulties and obstacles. This can only be resolved by the efforts and struggles of literary pioneers. This is also: literary pioneers have fulfilled their mission to the era.

In short, this era demands that its literary creators must live hard and write hard! The past era has never had the greatness and richness of today; the past has never had such an era, which grants creators the ability to write in the trend and earnestly and sincerely demands that they produce great works!

Literary Jottings

— Zai Qing

"Yellow Leaves" entering poetry are most evocative. After writing "Small Talk on Yellow Leaves," I have seen quite a few more. For example, Wu Shaoyun's "Wilted white lotus, people seeking society, desolate yellow leaves, magpies chirping in the village," "Autumn sound in yellow leaves, mountain shadow in twilight smoke," and "Bamboo light like sea blue clouds stopping, distant temple bell sounds heard several times. Walking to the end of Zhaoti's yellow leaf road, across the river, mountain color reaches the green door" (Lingyin Quan Taoguang) can all be said to be rare good lines. Recently, reading Ai Hongdao's poems, he also often uses "yellow leaves," but there are not many good lines. However, seeing his "Splitting Yellow Leaves to Stop Children from Crying," I am reminded that "yellow leaves" are also occasionally used in Buddhist books, but the meaning is different. Wu Linzheng and his uncle Shengbai painted clouds: "I also heard that my uncle does not send a single piece of paper to the capital, which is what he should do in his later years. Nowadays, important positions are fed up with meat, and a small amount of yellow leaves is not enough to stop children from crying. Why not simplify it to ensure purity? My uncle may mean this"? His meaning is the same as Yuan's poem, using "yellow leaves" as a metaphor for things that cannot satisfy people. Why do "yellow leaves" arouse poets' interest so much? Zhang Dai once thought like this:

Autumn leaves that are pure yellow are superior, variegated colors are next, and water red is next, the quality of the flowers, is beautiful here. But their haggard spirit is mostly in the midst of brilliance. Their red is fresh, taking wilting as a sign of contraction; their green is greasy, and purple is dark; their yellow is particularly rhythmic, but without green. The meaning of separation and fall is exhausted, and the flower is not there, is it what the gardener calls tender color? Old trees are beautiful in frost, not peaceful. Begging for it from Lang Seng at the beginning of summer was too early, unbearable for its worries; now it is thriving and glorious, enough to clap and praise. The sweetness of holding a crab and paddling for more than ten days, how can it be considered!

This can be seen in the eighth volume of "Notes," which shows that his understanding of "yellow leaves" is more profound than that of Li Jun and his like. The reason why "yellow leaves" are cherished by old poets is indeed due to the "nothing left" and "exhausted" mentioned here. A symbol of the extinction of life, a lament in the midst of the bleak autumn sound, is most likely to attack sentimental poets. As for those who do not look at "yellow leaves" with sentimental eyes, it is probably not in autumn, or perhaps only "imperfect beauty" can be used as an explanation. "Yellow leaves" are fundamentally not a sign of health. "Walking slowly and humming, the intention is unbearable," the sentimental poet's heart is mostly like this.

Descriptions and Content in Novels

— Ding Yishan

Speak of the general, not the details; look at the mainstream, not the tributaries.

A novel is a kind of descriptive and expressive social scientific reading material: the object it writes about is people, it describes the various phenomena of "people" striving and acting for individual survival and reproduction (or the continuation of the race), it describes the relationship between people and nature, society, and individuals. The expressions, hints, imitations, conflicts, cooperation, struggles, compromises, overcoming, surrender, or other similar qualities of these relationships. The causes or motives of these relationships are the desires of people that must be satisfied, and the results are either sad or happy, or a mixture of both. The difference between novels and other descriptive social sciences (such as history and geography) is that others appeal to our rational understanding, while novels appeal to both our rational understanding and our emotional appreciation.

A novel is not only an art to be appreciated, but it is also a kind of knowledge. What it describes and what it wants us to understand is the relative position of people in the system of nature, the relative position of groups and individuals in society, the motives of human activities, and the various relationships between these activities and the natural world, society, and the biological environment. Their concrete and invisible processes, psychological states, and their real and possible results. A novel can be a description of the phenomenon of a cross-section of human behavior, but more often it is a systematic description. It contains a historical nature, and allows for a considerable degree of imagination. It describes the past, and it also describes the future. It describes what it was and what it is more, and it describes what it will be and what it ought to be less, because readers can infer the future based on the past and present, and prophetic novels are not very reasonable.

Novels do not tell us doctrines and principles, like other descriptive social sciences, but they can implicitly or vaguely adopt doctrines and principles to make the phenomena described clearer, allowing readers to experience and discover them themselves. Its objective scope is the relationship between people and the natural, social, and biological environments, so its descriptions include natural landscapes, cities and villages, institutions and systems, individual behaviors and their characteristics, psychological states, and the sad or happy results of people's activities in various aspects. Many novels describe the relationship between people and the social environment (emphasizing institutional aspects) and the biological environment (emphasizing human aspects). For example, when describing fishermen by the sea and farmers on land, it is necessary to write about the struggle between people and nature, such as against wind, rain, drought, insect pests, etc. China's floods and droughts are most sufficient to express the struggle and relationship between farmers and the natural world. Although there are still no good works written with this kind of material, we can still understand this principle. The phenomenon of people in cold regions fighting with the geographical environment and the Dutch fighting with water especially shows the relationship between people and nature. The description of novels, in method and attitude, is not very different from other descriptive social sciences (such as history and geography). For example, the local color in novels means that novels contain geographical nature.

As for the method, novels use factual descriptions to make us aware of nature, society, and human nature. Sometimes they also try to explain, but it is different from what history, geography, and sociology do; the latter are all objective narratives and explanations, while novels contain reasonable imagination that does not violate the facts, because novels naturally include artistic components, and artistic components are to make the disguised facts have a greater effect on readers. Many novels have been made into movies, which makes us understand that novels are a description of a life in a certain place at a certain time, the aspect of life is not limited, and the size of the scope is not limited. Taking history, geography, and sociology for comparison, movies adapted from novels help us understand that novels appeal to our emotions and intellect. In fact, personnel matters are peculiar and abnormal, like the examples at both ends of the curve in statistics, and the experience, knowledge, and understanding of individuals are limited. Sometimes we read the peculiar places of personnel matters written in novels, sometimes it exceeds, sometimes it falls short. The truly peculiar personnel matters should not be viewed with pure subjective views. Except for the case study method in sociology, which is similar to novels, other social sciences all make generalized narratives and studies, which are abstract and conceptual: the description of novels is concrete, realistic, and close to our lives. Because of this, novels are the most able to express the various positions and psychology of people and are the most noticed and welcomed by us.

Tomorrow (20)

— Written by (Joseph Conrad), translated by Wu Xiangyu

They stood there like mutes. The old man, restless at the window, muttered to himself. Suddenly he shouted shrilly: "Bessan, I see you. I'll tell Harry."

She stirred as if to run away, but stopped, raising both hands to her cheeks. The little Haggipots shadow, blurred and big, stood motionless like a bronze man. Above them, the old man's voice quavered and scolded in the frantic night.

"Drive him away, my dear. He's only a vagrant. What you need is a good home of your own.

That fellow has no home—he's not like Harry. He'll never be Harry. Harry's coming back tomorrow. Do you hear? One more day," he mumbled more excitedly, "you don't have to be afraid—Harry's going to marry you."

His tone was sharp and frantic, echoing the howl of the wind blowing against the seawall outside.

"He has to marry you. I'll make him do it, if little," he swore, "I'll give him a shilling tomorrow to get out of here, and give all my belongings to you. I'll do it. Give it to you. Let him starve."

The window slammed shut again.

Harry took a long breath and took a step closer to Bessan. "So it's you—the girl who's been found," he said in a low voice. She didn't move, still half-turned away from him, her head pressed into the palms of her hands. "Honestly," he went on, a faint smile playing at the corners of his mouth. "I have a great desire to stay······"

His arms trembled terribly.

"Stay for a week," he said incredibly.

Her hands flew to cover her face.

He came up very close to her, gently gripping her wrists. She felt his breath on one ear.

"I'm in trouble—this time, perhaps only you can see it clearly. He tried to push her face away. She resisted. So he let her go, backing away a little, he asked, "Do you have any money? I have to leave now."

She nodded quickly and awkwardly, he waited, looking elsewhere, in another direction, she trembled all over, lowering her head, to find a pocket on her clothes.

"The money is here," she whispered. "Oh, go! For God's sake, go! If I had a little more—a little more—I would give it all to you, to make you forget—to make you forget everything."

He held out his hand. "Don't be afraid! I haven't forgotten one of you in the world. Some women have given me more than just money—but I'm a beggar now—you women often save me from trouble."

He strode to the window of the parlor, and in the dim light filtering out from the window, he looked at the coins in his palm. It was a half-sovereign (equal to half a pound). He put it in the bag. She stood there sideways, her head drooping, as if wounded, her arms hanging limply at her sides, as if dead.

"You can't buy me, and you can't be bought by anyone," he said.

He pressed his hat a little harder on his head, after which, she felt herself being lifted up by the embrace of his powerful arms. Her feet had left the ground; her head was raised; he poured down kisses on her face with silent but powerful passion, as if wanting to quickly capture her soul. He kissed her pale cheeks, her hard forehead, her long eyelashes, her dim lips; the ebb and flow and sighs of the tide, accompanied by the powerful embrace of his arms, came with a pity that overcame everything. It was like the sea, breaching the dyke protecting the townspeople's homes, sending a wave over her head. The wave passed! She staggered back, her shoulders against the wall, exhausted, just like after a storm and destruction, stranded in that place.

After a while, she reopened her eyes; her ears listened to the firm, orderly, triumphant footsteps walking away, her hands began to gather her clothes, her eyes always staring ahead. Suddenly she sped to the open door and went out into the darkness and desolate street.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talk

Opportunity to Boast

— Ma

The death of one's grandfather and mother is an opportunity to boast. Because one's grandfather and mother have died, hence there are obituaries and mourning announcements, and within these, the opportunity to boast arrives. How filial he was to his grandfather and mother, how he served them, and as for himself? How capable and great, he can use the deceased's tone to boast and brag, which is an excellent opportunity to boast.

Hearing of the death of a celebrity or important person is also an opportunity to boast. Regardless of whether he knows the celebrity or important person or not, he can sincerely make a funeral couplet or inscription, saying how the deceased "deeply relied on" him, how they "opened their hearts and stomachs" to him, how they "listened to him and followed his advice." Fortunately, the deceased is dead and cannot rise up to prove it. Let you boast to your heart's content, and bystanders cannot know. This is also an excellent opportunity to boast.

Holding a meeting is also an opportunity to boast, but boasting here also carries a bit of flattery. On the one hand, he boasts about himself, and on the other hand, he can also send sidelong glances to the deceased's family, which is originally a win-win situation, because the deceased is dead and can't be flattered, but his surviving family members can still be flattered, so the flattery has an aftertaste. This is also an excellent opportunity to boast and flatter.

However, you can boast as much as you want, but the first condition is that your grandfather and mother must die, or that a celebrity or important person must die. When they die, there is no proof. "Only the dead know what's in their stomachs," so you can boast at will, even if bystanders laugh their teeth off, he can ignore it. I have nothing to say about this kind of person, I can only deeply admire his thick skin and quick mind. In the past, I wrote two verses about boasting and flattery, which are now recorded below and offered as a gift.

Verse on Boasting

Asked what is boasting, its wonders are endless, let you say it traverses heaven and earth, originally form is emptiness.

Verse on Flattery

Flattery has many means, only one word is moderate, calling a cow or a horse is casual, the face is thick with iron armor ten layers.

After Watching the Public Performance of the John Drama Society

— Luo Ping

It's already been almost a year in a hurry.

A year ago, I and several comrades wanted to organize the John Drama Society and have a more meaningful public performance before Christmas, but in the end, due to various limitations of objective conditions and practical difficulties, the plan to organize the John Drama Society finally fell through.

However, I didn't expect that a year later today, thanks to the hard work of several classmates in the school, the John Drama Society was finally organized and finally gave a public performance. Being able to sprout this green bud in a very barren and dry desert, I felt an inexplicable gratification.

Mr. Sun Yu was invited to be the director, but because Mr. Sun Yu was busy with his work, the actual responsibility was borne by Mr. Huang Jiade.

The plays are three: Tian Han's "Death of a Famous Actor," Chen Bingquan's "Turtle," and Xiong Foxi's "Executioner."

It seems that there is no need to discuss the script of "Death of a Famous Actor" itself here. Here, the three acts have been changed to two acts, and with the efforts of several actors, the effect obtained is enough to be proud of. However, Qin Fuji, who played Master Yang, acted a little too much and became somewhat like a civilized drama. Wang Jinsheng's Liu Zhensheng was a little lacking. As for the female roles played by Lan Yeshen and Lan Yeqing, although they worked very hard later, it always felt a bit forced for men to dress up as women. When their affectations caused laughter from the audience, I couldn't help but think of the executioner's wife's dialogue in "Executioner": "Don't laugh, laughing makes people feel uncomfortable." Really, I felt uncomfortable in my heart, and at the same time, I felt a kind of shame and indignation. Friends, don't forget the black hand hiding behind you!

The second play is Chen Bingquan's self-written, self-directed, and self-performed "Turtle." In addition to his talent for acting, which is worthy of our praise, this script, which is purely about the jealousy and quarrels between young masters and young mistresses, is not as meaningful as "Death of a Famous Actor" and "Executioner." However, his demeanor is also too frivolous.

The last play is "Executioner," which is a relatively commendable one among Xiong Foxi's past plays. Perhaps because the stage was too large, the scenery here was too empty and monotonous. Mr. Zong Weigeng's lighting was very good here. Zhang Shirong, who played the "Executioner," was very serious. Zhu Wenji, who played the rent collector, was a little unfamiliar. Zhang Xunli worked very hard, and Lan Yeshen, who played the executioner's wife, was better than in "Death of a Famous Actor."

Of the effects received by the three plays, the last one was relatively more successful. And the national music played by the Xiaodian Orchestra did indeed evoke a leisurely nostalgic mood in people.

I understand the limitations of objective conditions and practical difficulties very clearly, but this public performance was able to achieve such satisfactory results. The hard work and spirit of the members are indeed worthy of our admiration.

Friends, I hope you cherish this sprout growing in the barren and dry desert: I am blessing you here!

Random Sketches of School Life, Part Two - Humor

Beard

— Chiyo-ko

Looking out from the window lattice at the high wall across the way, the pale yellow winter shadows were already slanting westward. I felt as if I had been sitting here all afternoon. The tobacco tin of "Buy cigarettes" beside my hand was gradually emptying, and I was idly stroking my chin when I was surprised to feel the prickly stubble. This was a new discovery. Finally, as if anticipating a major event for half a day, I searched out the broken mirror from the desk drawer.

An incomplete image appeared in the mirror. I thought someone else was standing behind me, but in this lonely small building, besides the lonely owner, only "Haru," huddled by the door, could guarantee that a stranger had never been seen. Still, distrustful, I turned my head to glance. On the wall hung a twenty-four-inch enlarged photograph, which was definitely not the figure in the mirror.

As if in a desert-like state of mind, I was suddenly disturbed. I stood up, flicked the cigarette ash, and searched out a photograph of myself from a pile of books covered in dust. Although I couldn't remember which year it was, I clearly remembered that it was taken on the same day as the twenty-four-inch enlarged photograph. Wasn't she young? How could the figure in the mirror have changed so much?

Sitting down again, I noticed that the sunlight on the wall had quietly disappeared. I had calculated thousands of times that it comes and goes quietly. I had even tried to trace its whereabouts, but where could I go to find it? This question has been缠绕ing me ever since. No, I should temporarily abandon it now and compare these two different shadows and images in detail.

This is truly a miracle; there is not the slightest resemblance in any part, so it's no wonder I thought someone else was standing behind me. Before one question was resolved, I was缠绕ed by a second. So I tried my best to explain to myself that one of these two must be me. First, I used the mirror to test it. When I pointed it at the wall, it reflected the twenty-four-inch enlarged photograph. When I pointed it at the corner of the door, it reflected "Haru's" weary state. When I pointed it at my clothes, it reflected the tattered cotton robe. Although this mirror

Page 18

is broken, it is still as accurate as before, reflecting a beautiful image of its owner. Then, the photograph must be wrong. I checked the back and saw a line of small words: "Taken in the spring of 1929 by the West Lake." What am I supposed to do? I clearly remember visiting Hangzhou in the spring of 1929. The twenty-four-inch enlarged photograph on the wall also has a background of swaying green willows. It can be determined that the figure in the mirror is me, and the photograph is also me. Involuntarily, I raised my hand to stroke my chin. Oh, that prickly beard, can you tell me where the me photographed in 1929 has gone? And where has the owner of that twenty-four-inch enlarged photograph gone? Hmph, did they come and go so quietly!

"Haru, do you know why you're barking?"

As it perked up its ears and barked wildly, the restaurant delivery man brought the night meal. The sky was completely dark. Naturally, the pale yellow winter shadows were impossible to trace. Very well, let everything be in darkness. I will not see that twenty-four-inch enlarged photograph, nor will I see these two different images and shadows. But I am still stroking the prickly beard! Old questions, new questions, will forever缠绕 me, even in the darkness.

Mad Woman

— Yu Jiong

The piercing cold wind howled, blowing against the few sailboats on the Wusong seashore. The vast seawater was constantly beaten by the cold wind, creating rhythmic sounds and ceaseless waves. Due to the excessive force of the sea wind, the waves crashed onto the pebbles. I enjoyed walking back and forth on the pebble road. During my free time, I would walk with my hands in my pockets, circling back and forth on the pebble road. Although the weather was cold, the beautiful scenery ultimately stirred up people's desire to stroll. One day, after dinner, the tide was rising and falling on the seashore. The road along the shore, which used to be covered with green grass, was now buried and the path was no longer visible. The setting sun cast a beautiful seascape even in winter. Countless ships, flying various flags, emitted whistling sounds, startling the fish hidden in the sea, which leaped and jumped, making quite a sight. Suddenly, a girl with a round face, wearing a green scarf, walked past me alone, strolling along the roadside. I shifted my gaze from the center of the sea and focused it on her. My heart began to feel uneasy. Why was someone walking along as if lost in thought? Could she be thinking of "suicide"? A suspicious thought lurked in my subconscious without being spoken when a familiar restaurant owner, Chen Ermazi, chased after her, his attitude quite nasty, closely following her footsteps, as if mumbling something. I became even more suspicious. Could he be trying to take advantage of her? Why would she let him chase her without saying a word? I could no longer contain my curiosity. Finally, I stopped the familiar restaurant owner, Chen Ermazi, and asked him why he was following this woman. Who exactly was she? Infinite anxiety was evident on her face, revealing how many secrets were hidden deep in her heart! In the moment that I stopped Chen Ermazi and chased after her again, her expression turned to relief, no longer as urgent as before. After Chen Ermazi explained that she owed him money for meals and gave a detailed account of her situation, I learned that she was a mad woman with a nervous condition, and that this so-called mad woman was actually a classmate who had entered the school with me more than half a year ago. Usually, because there were so many students, I hardly seemed to recognize her at all, until this day, when I learned her background.

From then on, after returning to school, I often heard about her past and her mad behavior in school. It was said that three years ago, she was the ninth concubine of Officer A in Sichuan. In this position, she was constantly subjected to the high pressure and arbitrary beatings from the eight higher-ranking wives. Moreover, when Officer A was promoted to commander, she was finally abandoned! Since then, after experiencing countless shocks in her life, her nerves had long been somewhat unclear! At school, she often let out loud cries and acted in ways that made people laugh. At these times, who could truly sympathize with her drifting fate? If someone truly comforted her, tears would stream from her eyes. We knew that she was not without reason or emotion, but that her reason and emotion were obscured and confused by the harsh reality!

Time is truly like flowing water. After the Japanese artillery fire destroyed C University, the whereabouts of this mad woman were said to be wandering everywhere. However, her deep, melodious, and mournful cries, mixed with the howling of the north wind, sometimes still echo in my ears.

New Books Sold as Waste Paper

— Song Yuan

Last year, bookstores selling new books by the pound was already alarming; now, bookstores are running prominent advertisements on newspaper front pages, proclaiming "New books sold as waste paper," which can't help but be shocking and heart-wrenching, lamenting the depression of the book industry to such an extent, and sensing the dim and lusterless future of culture.

Originally, cheap books are what scholars like most. In this era of rural economic bankruptcy and urban industrial depression, scholars have no choice but to buy books to satisfy their desire for knowledge, and the cost of books is equivalent to the cost of living. Cheap books mean a reduction in living expenses. Selling new books as waste paper should be considered a phenomenon that is very beneficial to scholars and the future of culture. However, we must know that bookstores are profit-making institutions for merchants, and their purpose in selling books is to make money. Now, running prominent advertisements, "New books sold as waste paper," clearly tells us, "No one is buying books, this is terrible!" Why is no one buying books? A simple sentence can answer: Scholars have no money. Since the cost of books for scholars is equivalent to the cost of living, and now that all industries are depressed, scholars are struggling to make a living. The cost of buying books beyond this living expense is naturally subject to a reduction policy, regardless. What the cultural cause relies on to promote, besides newspapers and magazines, is only new books. Now, scholars are not buying new books, so that "new books are sold as waste paper," the cultural future is truly worrying. It's hard to say that in the future, the new books of all bookstores will be sold as waste paper, and the cigarette shops and general stores will take the new books page by page and use them to wrap peanuts and groceries.

The new book industry has declared this year as the "magazine year," which has already told us that the sales of new books are not good, and only magazines are good business. Now, a certain bookstore is running a prominent advertisement, "New books sold as waste paper," and the purchasing power of new books is not as good as the purchasing power of magazines, which is further proof. However, in this so-called "magazine year," has the purchasing power of magazines increased compared to before? This is also a question worth paying attention to. As far as I know, the Commercial Press's "Eastern Miscellany" is an old brand with the largest sales, but this year it doesn't seem to be better than before. Also, literary magazines such as "Les Contemporains" and "Literature Quarterly" are also considered the best-selling publications, but this year they also don't seem to be better than last year. "Les Contemporains" magazine has even been suspended due to the poor business of the bookstore.

The society is in such a state of depression in all industries, the national economy is collapsing and bankrupting day by day, the purchasing power of new books is falling sharply, the cultural future is really terrible!

The military order was written on the spot and handed over in person. He hurriedly mounted his horse and advanced forward. Five hundred soldiers followed him with their swords. Suddenly, it was reported that the enemy troops were in a panic. Zhang Liao was the one who was wearing a crooked helmet and unloaded armor in front. A group of civil and military officials were haggard. Cao Cao didn't even wear a robe. With a roar of cannons, the mountains and valleys shook. Guan Gong stood on his horse with his sword in hand. Ambush soldiers intercepted and fought. He was so frightened that his heart was broken and he dared not escape. The Cao bandit knew that his feelings could be moved. He knelt down and begged bitterly with tears like a tide. Guan Gong couldn't bear it when he saw it. He had to stroke his long beard and look behind the formation. The bandit general took the opportunity to fly his horse over. Suddenly, he heard a thunderous roar and it was difficult to sit firmly. They all fell off their saddles and dared not run.

Page 21

Supplement of Shenbao in this city Film Special

Basic Qualifications of an Actress in the Words of Several Movie Moguls (Part Two)

David Ward Griffith, the great director, needs no introduction. Anyone who has seen a movie once or twice in the past twenty-five years knows Griffith's name. He "discovered" and single-handedly promoted several stars, including Mary Pickford, Douglas Fairbanks, Rudolph Valentino, Raoul Walsh, Van Dyke (also a famous director), Lionel Barrymore, Richard Barthelmess, Constance Talmadge, Norma Shearer, and others. He also gave Sylvia Sidney, Claudette Colbert, and Giselle Morlais their first screen tests. According to him, the most important qualification for a woman who wants to enter the modern film industry is talent. He said, "In the silent film era, a woman only needed to be beautiful on camera and agile in her movements to become an actress, but now, everything has changed. It is now doubly difficult to gain a foothold in the film industry compared to the past. Even the most insignificant parts must be given to experienced people because only experienced people know how to recite lines and make the film a complete, living thing. Therefore, it is extremely difficult for an inexperienced woman to enter the film industry now without any prior preparation. She should practice acting and dialogue in advance, and the best place to practice is in a small theater troupe. Hoping to become a movie star by working as an extra or in a minor role on a film set and rising step by step is never likely to succeed. What is needed on a film set now is vocal work. There is no better actress in sound films than Helen Hayes, but she had worked in the theater for many years before joining the film industry. Many other actresses who have become famous in the sound film industry also came from the theater, where they had already gained many essential experiences on the stage."

Lilyan Tashman's last director before her death was Chester Erskine. After Tashman's death, he praised her, saying, "She was the least temperamental and the easiest actress to direct. Although she was suffering from a serious illness, an illness that she knew would end her life, but which we did not know, she still worked every day from nine in the morning to five in the afternoon. She did not ask for any special treatment, and she worked harmoniously with other actors, from beginning to end, meticulously. Her death shook the entire film city." Erskine said of the selection of new actresses: "The first condition I look for in her is her appearance, that is, her appearance on camera. The second condition is her expression. If she has some personality, her expression when she speaks, her expression when she walks, and her expression when she sits and stands can all reveal her personality. The third condition is her ability. Ability cannot be discovered immediately, but once it is discovered, it must be considered when she is filming her second film. However, one thing that all women who want to join the film industry must understand is that being an actress is hard work. Those who think that becoming a movie star will bring endless wealth and glory are bound to be disappointed. A person who cannot devote themselves wholeheartedly is bound to fail miserably. Success requires years of work, and there is no shortcut."

Arthur Hopkins is a stage mogul who hired Katharine Hepburn to play in "Pride and Prejudice" at the Barrymore Theatre. He has the following opinions on how to choose actors: "The most important condition, of course, is general suitability for the work and special suitability for a particular role. Suitability includes appearance, speech, knowledge, and personality, etc. It is a mixture of various qualifications, not just one characteristic. Experience is desirable, but not essential. New talents can improve quickly under proper guidance if they have the qualities of an excellent actor. When rehearsing a play, the important roles are always cast first, and then the secondary roles are sought. Sometimes, you only need to read the script to know in advance who should play which role, without having to look for it."

There is also Eddie Dowling, a famous actor, producer, and director. He is currently directing a song and dance satire film. He said, "The first thing I look for is talent. People without talent are absolutely useless to us. But talent is not something you can see at a glance. For example, if there is a room full of new people you don't know, all you can do is pick out a few people with outstanding personalities or particularly transcendent attitudes. Beauty is certainly important, but it is secondary to talent. Many big stars are not very beautiful. A person with eight or nine points of beauty who has talent is much better than a person with ten points of beauty who has mediocre talent." From what has been said above, you can draw a rough and reliable conclusion: "Beauty, especially facial beauty, is very useful, but it is not absolutely essential. You must have other qualifications to succeed!" (The End)

Film Reviews

Review of "The Cremation Case"

— Stone Axe

Murder on The

Blackboard丨Nanjing Screening

After continuously showing many detective films, it seems that we have been fascinated by the great detective Sherlock Holmes. However, even if they are wonderful, we should be tired of watching them, let alone this "Cremation Case" after the "Goose Pond Tragedy"?

The simplicity of the story lies in the fact that it follows the old tune of others, making the corpses disappear without a trace, showing the strangeness of the strange. But unfortunately, we have seen enough of this old trick of destroying corpses. Moreover, this is not something that is reasonable, so in this respect, the script has lost its center of gravity. In addition, the director's skills are weak. While watching the play, we have to study it carefully, which is like being a detective again. This is because the whole play lacks a tense atmosphere, so you can think calmly while watching the play. I think the pretentiousness of the protagonist (Headmistress Withers, played by Edna May Oliver) is a bit too much.

In terms of exposition, it is too fragmented, and in terms of layout, it is so rigid. We are simply lost in the direction of the camera positions in several scenes in the cellar. When Inspector派拍剛 went out to take out a cigar to light, the first scene immediately followed by taking out the second cigar, we can easily see the negligence of the cut. The humor in the dialogue is not considered high-level, and the ending is a bit of a dog's tail.

As for the translation of the title "Murder on the Blackboard", the idea is still novel, but things such as poison, pistols, vases, and women's shoes are not uncommon in detective films. Moreover, here it is just that the name of the murderer is hidden in a short piece of music written on the blackboard, which is really very clumsy!

Audience Opinions

After Watching "Hundred Flowers Continent"

— Warrior

After watching "Hundred Flowers Continent," I couldn't help but celebrate for Tianyi. Really, "Hundred Flowers Continent," in terms of the consciousness of the script, has surpassed many of Tianyi's past films and is more meaningful than "The Deep Spring in the Red Chamber" and "Spring Night Serenade."

Although "Hundred Flowers Continent" still cannot escape the love disputes between men and women, it tells us that love is painful, love is the demon that buries our future, and the enemy that deceives our youth. We should abandon love and strive for the country and society to create our great future!

The purpose of the play is to convey such meaning, but because the playwright cannot correctly understand reality, and the director's technique is weak and powerless, it inevitably destroys the power of the whole play, which is a pity.

Among the actors, Chen Yumei's Zhou Yunxiang and Ye Qiuxin's Li Guifang worked harder, and Li Ying was also good, but a bit over the top.

The photography and scenery are good, but the subtitles are a bit too many.

In short, "Hundred Flowers Continent" should be a more successful and worthwhile work to watch compared to Tianyi Company's past works.

Movie Gossip

Twentieth Century Company plans to bring "The Mighty Barnum" to the screen, with Adolph Menjou playing Barnum's partner, Wallace Beery's wife Jean Harlow playing Mrs. Barnum, and Wallace Beery playing Barnum.

Mary Nolan's estate has now been fully accounted for, slightly exceeding 50,000 pounds.

MGM, in view of the business success of "Tarzan and His Mate," has specially invited Johnny Weissmuller and Maureen O'Sullivan to co-star in a new Tarzan film, and the location team has already set off for Africa for on-location filming.

Twentieth Century Company is now looking for a dog as amazing as Rin Tin Tin to co-star with Frank Lloyd in "The Call of the Wild," adapted from Jack London's novel.

Eddie Cantor's recently starring comedy "Kid Million" has been completed and will soon leave the United States for England.

After Watching "Shanghai Twenty-Four Hours"

— Xu Hairong

What we see here are fragments of Shanghai's darkness. The picture has lost its coherence, and everywhere shows stiffness and unnaturalness. Of course, we should forgive the director for the sake of the environment, it is not his fault!

However, this film still has its merits. At least, in terms of its content, we can see that it is a completely true portrayal, not an empty or ethereal one. The most successful part, I think, is several contrasts. For example, he writes that a child is seriously injured and is about to die, but he has no money to hire a doctor; and on the other hand, he writes that a comprador's wife pays a veterinary hospital twenty taels of silver. This contrast between people being worse than animals is so profound, moving, and powerful! Only a true portrayal can touch people's hearts, I think.

Although the picture has lost its coherence, each individual picture is still very good. For example, the street scenes of Shanghai reflected in the opening and ending scenes are so clear and beautiful!

Although the director has been heard to have some negligence, generally speaking, it is satisfactory. In many places, we can see his caution in handling this story. However, here he seems to only focus on the main characters, and neglects the rest of the actors, so that the plot of the whole film is a bit uncoordinated, such as Hu Wenlong, who can be said to have no expression at all. In addition, the extras in the dog racing arena and dance hall are also too stiff.

▲ "Model Youth" was completed yesterday, and the art department is rushing to produce subtitles.

▲ Nanhai beauty Hu Dieying came to Shanghai and stayed in Tianyi Village. After a short rest, she will work under the mercury lamp.

Movie Novel

Golden Lotus Tribulation (Have Heart) (Four)

— Uncle Min

Jimmy told Sally in the car that he would soon get a car like this. He said, "Do you know who's driving for you now? He's a big shot, James Farrell, the local manager." Sally's deep black eyes widened involuntarily, revealing a joyful light. She exclaimed softly, "Oh, Jimmy, have you been promoted?" Jimmy nodded, "Yes. Out of many people, I am the only one who has been promoted to local manager." At this time, Sally was happy for Jimmy and for herself, being able to be in the same car with this local manager, she temporarily forgot that she was a lame girl. But soon her dream was awakened, because Jimmy suddenly slammed on the brakes and said to Sally, "Do you know where this is? Roseland Ballroom. Let's go down and dance." Sally was shocked by what he said, and all the happiness disappeared. She could neither enter the ballroom nor tell him why. She couldn't say it on the one hand, and she sat still on the other, letting Jimmy urge her. Later, she suddenly thought of a plan, rejected his request to dance, and Jimmy seemed very satisfied and did not insist. Such an evening passed quickly and happily. When Jimmy sent Sally to her doorstep, Sally got out of the car by herself and told Jimmy not to get out. She said she wanted to stand and watch him drive the car away. But Jimmy refused. He said, "I must send you to your door. I have a special reason." Sally couldn't help but wonder, "What special reason do you have?" Jimmy said, "I think, if you are really happy, like you said, maybe you will let me kiss you for a moment." As he spoke, he looked at Sally with infinite hope. Sally hesitated for a while, then said, "Do you have to kiss people at the door?" Jimmy heard this, immediately hugged Sally in his arms, cried out "Angel," and kissed her. Sally was so happy with his kiss, and after a while, she pushed Jimmy away and said, "Okay, you go. I'll just stand here and wave goodbye to you." Jimmy looked at her reluctantly and said, "Okay, Angel, I'll see you tomorrow." He said and jumped into the car and drove away.

After Jimmy left, it wasn't until he returned to the company and put the car away that he found Sally's dog in his car. He jumped out of the car, and the dog followed him. It started barking. Jimmy hurriedly stopped it, but it was too late. The night watchman had already heard it and walked over. Jimmy quickly picked up the dog and ran into the company. He ran in the hallway and hid in a small room next to the hall, which was directly opposite the door of the cashier's room. No sooner said than done, the night watchman had already chased in. He had just walked to the door of the cashier's room when suddenly a person came out of the cashier's room with money. He walked behind the night watchman and hit him on the head with something. The night watchman immediately fell down. At this time, Jimmy's hand loosened, and the dog immediately窜了下去. It chased the robber. When the robber saw the dog coming up, he kicked it away. Jimmy quickly came out of the small room, walked through the hall, and wanted to lead the dog in. At this moment, the dog howled madly and flew straight out of another room, indeed being kicked out by the robber. Jimmy quickly hugged it and hid under the table. He looked around silently. After a while, he saw a hand stretching out from the room to turn off the light switch. The person turned off the light and ran away.

When the person reached out to turn off the switch, Jimmy saw a tattoo on his arm, which looked like a silver dollar. After Jimmy waited for the robber to escape, he immediately took Sally's dog and escaped. (To be continued)
